    SELECT [p].[ProductId], [p].[CategoryId], [p].[Description], [p].[ImagePath], [p].[Name], [p].[Price]
    FROM [Products] AS [p]
    WHERE [p].[ActiveStatus] = CAST(1 AS bit)
    ORDER BY [p].[Name]

) AS [p0]
INNER JOIN [Category] AS [c] ON [p0].[CategoryId] = [c].[CategoryId]
LEFT JOIN [Stock] AS [s] ON [p0].[ProductId] = [s].[ProductId]
LEFT JOIN [Reviews] AS [r] ON [p0].[ProductId] = [r].[ProductId]
LEFT JOIN [Reviews] AS [r0] ON [p0].[ProductId] = [r0].[ProductId]

    SELECT [p].[ProductId], [p].[CategoryId], [p].[Description], [p].[ImagePath], [p].[Name], [p].[Price]

) AS [p0]
INNER JOIN [Category] AS [c] ON [p0].[CategoryId] = [c].[CategoryId]
LEFT JOIN [Stock] AS [s] ON [p0].[ProductId] = [s].[ProductId]
LEFT JOIN [Reviews] AS [r] ON [p0].[ProductId] = [r].[ProductId]
LEFT JOIN [Reviews] AS [r0] ON [p0].[ProductId] = [r0].[ProductId]
